           <strong>
            <a href="https://www.bioalternatives.com/analyse-dexpression-de-genes/">
             <img alt="Biologie Moléculaire" class="alignnone wp-image-989 size-full" height="128" sizes="(max-width: 128px) 100vw, 128px" src="https://cdn-bneoicczbswi.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/TN_Biologie_Moleculaire.png" srcset="https://cdn-bneoicczbswi.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/TN_Biologie_Moleculaire.png 128w, https://cdn-bneoicczbswi.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/TN_Biologie_Moleculaire-80x80.png 80w, https://cdn-bneoicczbswi.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/TN_Biologie_Moleculaire-36x36.png 36w, https://cdn-bneoicczbswi.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/TN_Biologie_Moleculaire-120x120.png 120w" width="128"/>
            </a>
           </strong>
          </p>
          <p style="text-align: center;">
           <strong>
            Analyses transcriptomiques
           </strong>
          </p>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section class="av_textblock_section " itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="https://schema.org/CreativeWork">
         <div class="avia_textblock " itemprop="text" style="font-size:15px; ">
          <p style="text-align: center;">
           Service dédié à vos analyses transcriptomiques sur ARNm et microARN : RT-qPCR, PCRarrays, microarrays
          </p>
         </div>
        </section>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="flex_cell no_margin av_one_third avia-builder-el-42 el_after_av_cell_one_third avia-builder-el-last av-zero-padding " style="vertical-align:top; padding:0px; ">
       <div class="flex_cell_inner">
        <section class="av_textblock_section " itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="https://schema.org/CreativeWork">
         <div class="avia_textblock av_inherit_color " itemprop="text" style="font-size:22px; color:#000000; ">
          <p style="text-align: center;">
           <a href="https://www.bioalternatives.com/developpement-validation-tests-protocoles/">
            <img alt="TN_Tests_Et_Protocoles" class="aligncenter wp-image-15614 size-full" height="128" sizes="(max-width: 128px) 100vw, 128px" src="https://cdn-bneoicczbswi.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/TN_Tests_Et_Protocoles-3.png" srcset="https://cdn-bneoicczbswi.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/TN_Tests_Et_Protocoles-3.png 128w, https://cdn-bneoicczbswi.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/TN_Tests_Et_Protocoles-3-80x80.png 80w, https://cdn-bneoicczbswi.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/TN_Tests_Et_Protocoles-3-125x125.png 125w, https://cdn-bneoicczbswi.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/TN_Tests_Et_Protocoles-3-36x36.png 36w, https://cdn-bneoicczbswi.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/TN_Tests_Et_Protocoles-3-120x120.png 120w" width="128"/>
           </a>
          </p>
          <p style="text-align: center;">
           <strong>
            Développement et validation de tests
            <em>
             in vitro
            </em>
           </strong>
          </p>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section class="av_textblock_section " itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="https://schema.org/CreativeWork">
         <div class="avia_textblock " itemprop="text" style="font-size:15px; ">
          <p style="text-align: center;">
           Des prestations dédiées au développement, à l’optimisation et à la validation
           <br/>
           de nouvelles méthodes d’analyse ou protocoles de recherche
          </p>
         </div>
        </section>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
